\DoxyCodeLine{02768\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02769\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NAME\ curl\_global\_sslset()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02770\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02771\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02772\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02773\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ built\ with\ multiple\ SSL\ backends,\ curl\_global\_sslset()\ allows\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02774\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ choose\ one.\ This\ function\ can\ only\ be\ called\ once,\ and\ it\ must\ be\ called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02775\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ *before*\ curl\_global\_init().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02776\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02777\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ backend\ can\ be\ identified\ by\ the\ id\ (e.g.\ CURLSSLBACKEND\_OPENSSL).\ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02778\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ backend\ can\ also\ be\ specified\ via\ the\ name\ parameter\ (passing\ -\/1\ as\ id).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02779\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ both\ id\ and\ name\ are\ specified,\ the\ name\ will\ be\ ignored.\ If\ neither\ id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02780\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ nor\ name\ are\ specified,\ the\ function\ will\ fail\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02781\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ CURLSSLSET\_UNKNOWN\_BACKEND\ and\ set\ the\ "{}avail"{}\ pointer\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02782\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NULL-\/terminated\ list\ of\ available\ backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02783\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02784\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Upon\ success,\ the\ function\ returns\ CURLSSLSET\_OK.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02785\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02789\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
